./cluster/cluster_pattern.html:112:					HA Mode 
./cluster/cluster_pattern.html:117:					<span style="font-weight:bold;">主备模式：</span>双机热备，主设备处于发布服务状态，备设备不工作，备设备如果发现主设备故障，接替主设备继续提供服务。
./cluster/cluster_pattern.html:122:					<span style="font-weight:bold;">高可用集群模式：</span>支持多台设备组建集群，集群中的不同设备可发布不同的服务，并且互相监视健康状态，如果其中的一台设备故障，其发布的服务会被集群中的其他设备接替。
./cluster/cluster_pattern.html:127:					<span style="font-weight:bold;">高性能集群模式：</span>支持多台设备组建集群，高性能。

./cluster/cluster_pattern.html:170:		<span class="obj_title">Active-standby </span>
./cluster/cluster_pattern.html:171:		<p style="text-indent: 2em;">There are two units involved. One is Active and provides HA service, while the other is Standby and not provides HA service. When active unit fails, the standby unit changes to Active and takes over the service. </p>
./cluster/cluster_pattern.html:173:		<p style="text-indent: 2em;">In this mode, all of the features of an ADC are available. </p>
./cluster/cluster_pattern.html:176:		<span class="obj_title">High-availability cluster </span>
./cluster/cluster_pattern.html:177:		<p style="text-indent: 2em;">There are up to 16 ADC units involved. A service is running on one of the units, the Active unit, a second unit will be elected to work as Standby unit. When the Active unit fails, the standby unit changes to Active and takes over the service. However, services on different ADC units can run concurrently, as backups for one another when necessary. </p>
./cluster/cluster_pattern.html:181:		<span class="obj_title">High-performance cluster </span>
./cluster/cluster_pattern.html:182:		<p style="text-indent: 2em;">There are up to 8 ADC units involved. With link aggregation configured on the switch connected to the HA interface, data of a service will be assigned to each unit in the cluster to handle, dramatically improving performance. When there is any unit exits the cluster or any new unit is joined to the cluster, traffic will be fairly assigned among the clustered united to ensure business continuity. </p>
./cluster/cluster_pattern.html:184:		<p style="text-indent: 2em;">This mode is chosen for server load balancing, therefore, link load, IPv6, SSL connection multiplexing and dynamically routing are not supported. </p>
